1.2 Real-World Protection Test\n\n**1.2.1 Test Methodology**\n```\nReal-World Protection Test:\nв”ңв”Җ Test Duration\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 4-week testing period\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Continuous monitoring\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Real-world attack scenarios\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Live threat feeds\nв”ңв”Җ Test Samples\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 200+ zero-day attack URLs\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 100+ exploit kit URLs\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 50+ phishing URLs\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Real-time threat intelligence\nв”ңв”Җ Test Metrics\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Protection rate: Target >99.5%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ False positive rate: Target <0.1%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Detection time: Target <100ms\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Block rate: Target >95%\nв”ңв”Җ Scoring\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 6.0 points: Excellent (вүҘ99.5%)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 5.5 points: Very Good (вүҘ99.0%)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 5.0 points: Good (вүҘ98.5%)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 4.5 points: Satisfactory (вүҘ98.0%)\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ 4.0 points: Standard (вүҘ97.5%)\nв””в”Җ SENTINEL Target\n   в”ңв”Җ Protection rate: 99.8%\n   в”ңв”Җ False positive rate: 0.05%\n   в”ңв”Җ Detection time: 50ms\n   в””в”Җ Score: 6.0 points (Excellent)\n```\n\n**1.2.2 Test Scenarios**\n```\nReal-World Test Scenarios:\nв”ңв”Җ Drive-by Downloads\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Malicious websites hosting exploit kits\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Automatic download and execution\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Zero-day exploits\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Target: 100% protection\nв”ңв”Җ Phishing Attacks\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Fake login pages\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Credential harvesting\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Social engineering\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Target: 99.5% protection\nв”ңв”Җ Malvertising\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Malicious advertisements\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Ad network compromise\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Redirect chains\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Target: 99.5% protection\nв””в”Җ Social Engineering\n   в”ңв”Җ Fake software downloads\n   в”ңв”Җ Fake updates\n   в”ңв”Җ Tech support scams\n   в””в”Җ Target: 99% protection\n```\n\n### 1.3 Malware Protection Test\n\n**1.3.1 Test Methodology**\n```\nMalware Protection Test:\nв”ңв”Җ Test Duration\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 4-week testing period\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ On-demand scanning\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ On-access scanning\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Scheduled scanning\nв”ңв”Җ Test Samples\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 10,000+ malware samples\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 5,000+ zero-day samples\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 2,000+ polymorphic samples\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ 1,000+ fileless samples\nв”ңв”Җ Test Metrics\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Detection rate: Target >99.8%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ False positive rate: Target <0.05%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Scan speed: Target >10 GB/s\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ System impact: Target <2%\nв”ңв”Җ Scoring\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 6.0 points: Excellent (вүҘ99.8%)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 5.5 points: Very Good (вүҘ99.5%)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 5.0 points: Good (вүҘ99.0%)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 4.5 points: Satisfactory (вүҘ98.5%)\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ 4.0 points: Standard (вүҘ98.0%)\nв””в”Җ SENTINEL Target\n   в”ңв”Җ Detection rate: 99.9%\n   в”ңв”Җ False positive rate: 0.03%\n   в”ңв”Җ Scan speed: 15 GB/s\n   в””в”Җ Score: 6.0 points (Excellent)\n```\n\n**1.3.2 Malware Categories**\n```\nMalware Categories Tested:\nв”ңв”Җ Ransomware\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 2,000+ ransomware samples\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Encryption-based ransomware\nв”Ӯ Methodology**\n```\nPerformance Test:\nв”ңв”Җ Test Duration\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 4-week testing period\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Continuous performance monitoring\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ System impact measurement\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ <2s\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ File copy impact: Target <5%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ File download impact: Target <5%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Website launch impact: Target <5%\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Software installation impact: Target <5%\nв”ңв”Җ   в””в”Җ Score: 6.0 points (Excellent)\n```\n\n**1.5.2 Usability Scenarios**\n```\nUsability Test Scenarios:\nв”ңв”Җ False Positive Testing\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 10,000+ benign files\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Common 2.2 Real-World Protection Test\n\n**2.2.1 Test Methodology**\n```\nAV-Comparatives Real-World Protection Test:\nв”ңв”Җ Test Duration\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 2-month testing period\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Continuous monitoring\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Real-world attack scenarios\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Live threat feeds\nв”ңв”Җ Test Samples\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 500+ real-world attack scenarios\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ 200+ exploit kit URLs\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ required"\nв””в”Җ Status Details\n   в”ңв”Җ Real-Time Protection: ON/OFF\n   в”ңв”Җ Last Scan: X hours ago\n   в”ңв”Җ Threats Blocked: X this month\n   в”ңв”Җ System Health: EXCELLENT/GOOD/FAIR/POOR\n   в””в”Җ Next Scheduled Scan: X hours from now\n```\n\n### 1.3 Minimalist Design\n\n**1.3.1 Design Principles**\n```\nMinimalist Design Principles:\nв”ңв”Җ Visual Simplicity\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Clean, uncluttered interface\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Consistent color scheme (green, white, gray)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Clear typography hierarchy\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Generous white space\nв”ңв”Җ Information Architecture\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Progressive disclosure\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Group related information\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Use icons for quick recognition\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Clear visual hierarchy\nв”ңв”Җ Interaction Design\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ One-click actions\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Clear call-to-action buttons\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Intuitive navigation\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Consistent interaction patterns\nв””в”Җ Accessibility\n   в”ңв”Җ Keyboard navigation\n   в”ңв”Җ Screen reader support\n   в”ңв”Җ High contrast mode\n   в””в”Җ Font size adjustment\n```\n\n**1.3.2 Color Scheme**\n```\nColor Scheme:\nв”ңв”Җ Primary Colors\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Sentinel Green: #00C853 (Success, Protected)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Warning Yellow: #FFD600 (Warnings, Attention)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Alert Orange: #FF6D00 (Alerts, Action Required)\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Critical Red: #D50000 (Critical, Immediate Action)\nв”ңв”Җ Neutral Colors\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ White: #FFFFFF (Background, Primary Text)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Light Gray: #F5F5F5 (Secondary Background)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Medium Gray: #9E9E9E (Secondary Text)\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Dark Gray: #424242 (Primary Text on Light Background)\nв”ңв”Җ Accent Colors\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Gaming Blue: #2979FF (Gaming Mode)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Privacy Purple: #651FFF (Privacy Features)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Primary Text: #FFFFFF\n   в””в”Җ Secondary Text: #B0B0B0\n```\n\n### 1.4 Intelligent Notifications\n\n**1.4.1 Notification Philosophy**\n```\nIntelligent Notification Philosophy:\nв”ңв”Җ Notification Categories\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Critical: Immediate action required (show immediately)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Important: Action recommended (show within 1 hour)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Informational: Status updates (show in activity log)\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Background: Silent logging (no notification)\nв”ңв”Җ Notification Frequency\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Critical: As needed, no throttling\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Important: Maximum 1 per hour\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Informational: Maximum 1 per day\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Background: No notifications\nв”ңв”Җ Notification Content\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Clear, concise message\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Actionable recommendation\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Contextual information\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ One-click resolution\nв””в”Җ Notification Dismissal\n   в”ңв”Җ Dismiss with action\n   в”ңв”Җ Snooze for later\n   в”ңв”Җ Learn more option\n   в””в”Җ Don\'t show again (for informational)\n```\n\n**1.4.2 Notification Examples**\n```\nNotification Examples:\nв”ңв”Җ Critical Notifications\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "CRITICAL: Ransomware detected and blocked. Your files are safe."\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "CRITICAL: System compromise detected. Immediate action required."\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ "CRITICAL: Unauthorized access attempt blocked. Review security settings."\nв”ңв”Җ Important Notifications\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "Threat detected and blocked: Trojan.GenericKD.46789234"\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "Security update available. Install now for optimal protection."\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ "Suspicious activity detected. Review recent system changes."\nв”ңв”Җ Informational Notifications\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "Full scan completed. No threats found."\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "Virus definitions updated successfully."\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ "Gaming mode enabled. Performance optimized for gaming."\nв””в”Җ Background Notifications (Activity Log Only)\n   в”ңв”Җ "File scanned: document.pdf"\n   в”ңв”Җ "Website accessed: example.com"\n   в””в”Җ "Process monitored: chrome.exe"\n```\n\n## 2. Quick Actions**\n```\nQuick Actions:\nв”ңв”Җ Scan Actions\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ [Quick Scan] - Scan common locations (~5 minutes)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ [Full Scan] - Scan entire system (~2 hours)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ [Custom Scan] - Select specific locations\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ [Scan Now] - Start immediate scan\nв”ңв”Җ Protection Actions\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ [Enable Protection] - Turn on real-time protection\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ [Disable Protection] - Turn off real-time protection\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ [Enable Gaming Mode] - Optimize for gaming\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ [Disable Gaming Mode] - Return to normal mode\nв”ңв”Җ Update Actions\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ [Check for Updates] - Check for virus definition updates\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ [Update Now] - Install available updates\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ [Enable Auto-Update] - Turn on automatic updates\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ [Disable Auto-Update] - Turn off automatic updates\nв””в”Җ Settings Actions\n   в”ңв”Җ [Open Settings] - Access all settings\n   в”ңв”Җ [Reset to Defaults] - Reset all settings to defaults\n   в”ңв”Җ [Export Settings] - Export settings to file\n   в””в”Җ [Import Settings] - Import settings from file\n```\n\n### 2.3 Automated Protection\n\n**2.3.1 Automatic Threat Handling**\n```\nAutomatic Threat Handling:\nв”ңв”Җ Threat Detection\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Detect threat: AI + signature + behavioral analysis\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Classify threat: Severity (Low, Medium, High, Critical)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Determine action: Quarantine, Delete, Ignore\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Execute action: Automatic (no user intervention)\nв”ңв”Җ Threat Response\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Low severity: Log only, no action\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Medium severity: Quarantine, notify user\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ High severity: Quarantine, notify user immediately\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Critical severity: Delete, notify user immediately\nв”ңв”Җ User Notification\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Low severity: No notification (activity log only)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Medium severity: Informational notification\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ High severity: Important notification\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Critical severity: Critical notification\nв””в”Җ User Action\n   в”ңв”Җ Low severity: No action required\n   в”ңв”Җ Medium severity: Review recommended\n   в”ңв”Җ High severity: Review required\n   в””в”Җ Critical severity: Immediate action required\n```\n\n**2.3.2 Automatic Updates**\n```\nAutomatic Updates:\nв”ңв”Җ Update Types\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Virus definitions: Daily, automatic\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Engine updates: Weekly, automatic\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Feature updates: Monthly, automatic\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Major updates: Quarterly, user confirmation\nв”ңв”Җ Update Schedule\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Virus definitions: Check every 4 hours\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Engine updates: Check every 24 hours\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Feature updates: Check every 7 days\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Major updates: Check every 30 days\nв”ңв”Җ Update Installation\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Virus definitions: Install immediately\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Engine updates: Install when idle\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Feature updates: Install when idle\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Major updates: Ask user, install when ready\nв””в”Җ Update Notifications\n   в”ңв”Җ Virus definitions: No notification\n   в”ңв”Җ Engine updates: Informational notification\n   в”ңв”Җ Feature updates: Important notification\n   в””в”Җ Major updates: Critical notification\n```\n\n## 3. 3.2 Security Recommendations\n\n**3.2.1 Security Recommendations Engine**\n```\nSecurity Recommendations:\nв”ңв”Җ Vulnerability Detection\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Outdated software: Update recommended\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Missing security patches: Install recommended\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Weak passwords: Change recommended\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Insecure settings: Configure recommended\nв”ңв”Җ Configuration Optimization\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Real-time protection: Ensure enabled\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Automatic updates: Ensure enabled\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Scheduled scans: Ensure configured\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Firewall: Ensure enabled\nв”ңв”Җ Threat Prevention\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Phishing protection: Enable recommended\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Ransomware protection: Enable recommended\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Network protection: Enable recommended\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Browser protection: Enable recommended\nв””в”Җ Security Best Practices\n   в”ңв”Җ Two-factor authentication: Enable recommended\n   в”ңв”Җ Backup: Configure recommended\n   в”ңв”Җ Encryption: Enable recommended\n   в””в”Җ Privacy settings: Review recommended\n```\n\n**3.2.2 Recommendation Examples**\n```\nSecurity Recommendation Examples:\nв”ңв”Җ High Priority\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "Your Windows is outdated. Update now for security patches."\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "Real-time protection is disabled. Enable for optimal protection."\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "Critical security vulnerability detected. Update immediately."\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ "Weak password detected. Change to a stronger password."\nв”ңв”Җ Medium Priority\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "Automatic updates are disabled. Enable for latest protection."\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "Scheduled scans are not configured. Set up regular scans."\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "Firewall is disabled. Enable for network protection."\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ "Browser protection is disabled. Enable for web security."\nв””в”Җ Low Priority\n   в”ңв”Җ "Consider enabling two-factor authentication for added security."\n   в”ңв”Җ "Review your privacy settings for optimal protection."\n   в”ңв”Җ "Set up regular backups for data protection."\n   в””в”Җ "Enable ransomware protection for file security."\n```\n\n### 3.3 Performance Recommendations\n\n**3.3.1 Performance Optimization Engine**\n```\nPerformance Recommendations:\nв”ңв”Җ Resource Optimization\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ High CPU usage: Optimize settings\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ High memory usage: Optimize settings\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ High disk I/O: Optimize settings\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ High network usage: Optimize settings\nв”ңв”Җ Gaming Optimization\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Gaming mode not enabled: Enable for better performance\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ High background activity: Optimize for gaming\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Network latency detected: Optimize network settings\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ FPS drops detected: Optimize system settings\nв”ңв”Җ System Optimization\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Slow boot time: Optimize startup programs\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Slow application launch: Optimize system settings\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Slow file operations: Optimize disk settings\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ System slowdown detected: Optimize overall performance\nв””в”Җ Battery Optimization\n   в”ңв”Җ High battery drain: Optimize power settings\n   в”ңв”Җ Background activity detected: Optimize for battery life\n   в””в”Җ Power-hungry apps detected: Optimize app settings\n```\n\n**3.3.2 Recommendation Examples**\n```\nPerformance Recommendation Examples:\nв”ңв”Җ High Priority\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "High CPU usage detected. Optimize settings for better performance."\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "Gaming mode is disabled. Enable for better gaming performance."\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "System slowdown detected. Optimize for better performance."\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ "High battery drain detected. Optimize power settings."\nв”ңв”Җ Medium Priority\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "Background activity is high. Optimize for better performance."\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "Network latency detected. Optimize network settings."\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "FPS drops detected. Optimize gaming settings."\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ "Slow boot time detected. Optimize startup programs."\nв””в”Җ Low Priority\n   в”ңв”Җ "Consider enabling RAM defolding for better gaming performance."\n   в”ңв”Җ "Review background processes for optimization opportunities."\n   в”ңв”Җ "Optimize disk settings for faster file operations."\n   в””в”Җ "Review power settings for better battery life."\n```\n\n### 3.4 Privacy Recommendations\n\n**3.4.1 Privacy Protection Engine**\n```\nPrivacy Recommendations:\nв”ңв”Җ Data Collection Control\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Telemetry enabled: Disable for better privacy\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Crash reports enabled: Disable for better privacy\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Usage statistics enabled: Disable for better privacy\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Location services enabled: Review for privacy\nв”ңв”Җ Application Privacy\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Apps with excessive permissions: Review permissions\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Apps accessing sensitive data: Review access\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Apps with network access: Review network activity\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Apps with background activity: Review background access\nв”ңв”Җ Browser Privacy\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Tracking cookies detected: Clear cookies\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Browser fingerprinting detected: Enable protection\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Ad tracking detected: Enable ad blocking\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Privacy extensions recommended: Install extensions\nв””в”Җ System Privacy\n   в”ңв”Җ Location services enabled: Review for privacy\n   в”ңв”Җ Camera access enabled: Review for privacy\n   в”ңв”Җ Microphone access enabled: Review for privacy\n   в””в”Җ File access enabled: Review for privacy\n```\n\n**3.4.2 Recommendation Examples**\n```\nPrivacy Recommendation Examples:\nв”ңв”Җ High Priority\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "Telemetry is enabled. Disable for better privacy."\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "Apps with excessive permissions detected. Review permissions."\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "Tracking cookies detected. Clear cookies for better privacy."\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ "Location services are enabled. Review for privacy."\nв”ңв”Җ Medium Priority\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "Crash reports are enabled. Disable for better privacy."\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "Browser fingerprinting detected. Enable protection."\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ "Ad tracking detected. Enable ad blocking."\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ "Privacy extensions recommended. Install for better privacy."\nв””в”Җ Low Priority\n   в”ңв”Җ "Consider using a VPN for better privacy."\n   в”ңв”Җ "Review app permissions for privacy optimization."\n   в”ңв”Җ "Enable private browsing for better privacy."\n   в””в”Җ "Review system privacy settings for optimization."\n```\n\n## 4. Customizable Protection Levels\n\n### 4.1 Protection Level Architecture\n\n```\nCustomizable Protection Unique Advantage)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Anti-cheat compatibility layer\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Integrity proof generation\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Zero-scan mode activation\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Support for Vanguard, EAC, BattlEye\nв”ңв”Җ Anti-DDoS Shield (Gaming - Unique Advantage)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Traffic monitoring and analysis\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Attack detection algorithms\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Traffic routing optimization\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Basic privacy protection\nв”ңв”Җ Basic User Interface\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Zero-knowledge interface\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ One-click protection toggle\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Real-time status display\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Basic settings configuration\nв””в”Җ Core Security Features\n   в”ңв”Җ Real-time file scanning\n   в”ңв”Җ Process monitoring\n   в”ңв”Җ Basic network protection\n   в””в”Җ Threat quarantine and removal\n```\n\n### 1.2 MVP Technical Architecture\n\n**1.2.1 System Architecture**\n```\nMVP System Architecture:\nв”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ\nв”Ӯ                    SENTINEL MVP Architecture                 в”Ӯ\nв”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө\nв”Ӯ  User Interface Layer                                       в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Desktop Application (Electron + React)                 в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ System Tray Application                                в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Web Dashboard (Optional)                               в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Mobile App (Optional - Phase 2)                        в”Ӯ\nв”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө\nв”Ӯ  Service Layer                                              в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Protection Service (Windows Service)                   в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Update Service (Windows Service)                       в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Gaming Service (Windows Service)                       в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ UI Communication Service (Named Pipes)                 в”Ӯ\nв”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө\nв”Ӯ  Core Engine Layer                                          в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Ring -1 Hypervisor (Rust)                              в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ AI Engine (Python + PyTorch)                           в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Detection Engine (C++ + YARA)                          в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Gaming Engine (C++)                                    в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Network Engine (Rust)                                  в”Ӯ\nв”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө\nв”Ӯ  Data Layer                                                 в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ SQLite Database (Local)                                в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Signature Database (Encrypted)                         в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ AI Model Files (Encrypted)                             в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Configuration Files (Encrypted)                        в”Ӯ\nв”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө\nв”Ӯ  Hardware Abstraction Layer                                 в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ NPU Interface (Intel NPU, AMD NPU, Apple Neural Engine)в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ TPM Interface                                           в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Secure Boot Interface                                  в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Hardware Security Module (HSM) Interface               в”Ӯ\nв””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ\n```\n\n**1.2.2 Technology Stack**\n```\nTechnology Stack:\nв”ңв”Җ Core Components\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Ring -1 Hypervisor: Rust (memory-safe, low-level)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ AI Engine: Python 3.11 + PyTorch 2.0\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Detection Engine: C++23 + YARA 4.3\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Gaming Engine: C++23\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Network Engine: Rust (Tokio async runtime)\nв”ңв”Җ User Interface\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Desktop App: Electron 28 + React 18 + TypeScript\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ UI Framework: Material-UI (MUI) 5\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ State Management: Redux Toolkit\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Build Tool: Vite 5\nв”ңв”Җ Services\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Windows Services: C++23 (Win32 API)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ IPC: Named Pipes (Windows)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Logging: spdlog (C++) / loguru (Rust)\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Configuration: TOML + serde (Rust)\nв”ңв”Җ Data Storage\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Local Database: SQLite 3\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ ORM: Diesel (Rust) / SQLiteCpp (C++)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Encryption: libsodium (post-quantum ready)\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Backup: Custom backup system\nв”ңв”Җ Build & Deployment\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Build System: CMake (C++) / Cargo (Rust)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Package Manager: vcpkg (C++) / Cargo (Rust)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ CI/CD: GitHub Actions\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Installer: WiX Toolset (MSI)\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Code Signing: DigiCert EV Code Signing Certificate\nв””в”Җ Testing\n   в”ңв”Җ Unit Testing: Google Test (C++) / Rust Testing\n   в”ңв”Җ Integration Testing: Custom framework\n   в”ңв”Җ Performance Testing: BenchmarkDotNet (C++)\n   в””в”Җ Security Testing: AFL++ fuzzing\n```\n\n### 1.3 MVP Development Phases\n\n**Phase 1: Foundation (Months 1-3)**\n```\nFoundation Phase:\nв”ңв”Җ Month 1: Team Setup & Infrastructure\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Recruit core team (5 people)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Set up development environment\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Configure CI/CD pipeline\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Set up code repositories\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Establish в””в”Җ Create hypervisor API\nв”ңв”Җ Month 3: Basic Detection Engine\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Implement YARA signature matching\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Create signature database\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Implement file scanning\nв”Ӯ Implement scoring algorithm\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Create threat classification\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Optimize detection performance\nв””в”Җ Deliverables:\n   в”ңв”Җ Working AI detection engine\n   в”ңв”Җ Behavioral False Positive Rate: <0.1%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ CPU Usage: <3%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ RAM Usage: <600MB\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Boot Time Impact: <3s\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Crash Rate: <0.1%\nв”ңв”Җ Gaming Metrics\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Anti-Cheat Compatibility: >95%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ FPS Improvement: >15%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Latency Reduction: >50%\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ DDoS Protection: >90%\nв”ңв”Җ User Metrics\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Installation Success Rate: >98%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ User Satisfaction: >85%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Support Ticket Rate: <5%\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Churn Rate: <10%\nв””в”Җ Business Metrics\n   в”ңв”Җ User Acquisition: >10,000 users\n   в”ңв”Җ Conversion Rate: >5%\n   в”ңв”Җ Revenue: >$100K/month\n   в””в”Җ Market Feedback: Positive\n```\n\n## 2. Technical Architecture for Implementation\n\n### 2.1 System Components\n\n**2.1.1 Core Components**\n```\nCore Components Architecture:\nв”ңв”Җ Hypervisor Component (Ring -1)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ hypervisor_core.dll (Rust)\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Memory management\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Process monitoring\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Write-blocking\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Hardware abstraction\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ hypervisor_driver.sys (C++)\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Kernel-level operations\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Hardware access\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ System calls\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ hypervisor_api.lib (C++)\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ API for other components\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Communication layer\nв”Ӯ     в””в”Җ Error handling\nв”ңв”Җ Detection Component (Ring 0)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ detection_engine.dll (C++)\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Signature matching (YARA)\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Heuristic analysis\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Behavioral analysis\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Threat scoring\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ ai_engine.dll (Python)\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Model inference\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Anomaly detection\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Pattern recognition\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Model updates\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ signature_db.sqlite (Encrypted)\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Virus signatures\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ YARA rules\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Heuristic patterns\nв”Ӯ     в””в”Җ Behavioral patterns\nв”ңв”Җ Gaming Component (Ring 0)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ gaming_engine.dll (C++)\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Trusted Handshake\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Anti-DDoS Shield\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ RAM Defolding\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Performance optimization\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ anti_cheat_compat.dll (C++)\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Vanguard compatibility\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ EAC compatibility\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ BattlEye compatibility\nв”Ӯ   в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Generic anti-cheat support\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ game_profiles.db (Encrypted)\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Game-specific settings\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Performance profiles\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Anti-cheat rules\nв”Ӯ     в””в”Җ Optimization settings\nв””в”Җ Network Component (Ring 0)\n   в”ңв”Җ network_engine.dll (Rust)\n   в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Traffic monitoring\n   в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Attack detection\n   в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Traffic routing\n   в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Privacy protection\n   в”ңв”Җ firewall_rules.db (Encrypted)\n   в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Firewall rules\n   в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Traffic policies\n   в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Privacy settings\n   в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Network profiles\n   в””в”Җ network_monitor.sys (C++)\n      в”ңв”Җ Packet capture\n      в”ңв”Җ Traffic analysis\n      в”ңв”Җ Protocol inspection\n      в””в”Җ Network filtering\n```\n\n**2.1.2 Service Architecture**\n```\nService Architecture:\nв”ңв”Җ Windows Services\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ SentinelProtectionService.exe\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Manages real-time protection\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Coordinates detection components\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Handles threat responses\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Communicates with UI\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ SentinelUpdateService.exe\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Manages signature updates\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Handles engine updates\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Downloads updates securely\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Installs updates safely\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ SentinelGamingService.exe\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Manages gaming features\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Detects game launches\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Activates gaming mode\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Optimizes performance\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ SentinelUIService.exe\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Handles UI communication\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Manages user settings\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Provides status updates\nв”Ӯ     в””в”Җ Handles user requests\nв”ңв”Җ Background Processes\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ SentinelScanner.exe\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Performs scheduled scans\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Manages scan queues\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Reports scan results\nв”Ӯ   в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Optimizes scan performance\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ SentinelAIWorker.exe\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Runs AI inference\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Updates AI models\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Performs federated learning\nв”Ӯ   в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Optimizes AI performance\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ SentinelNetworkMonitor.exe\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Monitors network traffic\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Detects network threats\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Blocks malicious traffic\nв”Ӯ     в””в”Җ Reports network events\nв””в”Җ System Tray Application\n   в”ңв”Җ SentinelTray.exe\n   в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Displays system tray icon\n   в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Shows protection status\n   в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Provides quick actions\n   в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Handles notifications\n   в””в”Җ SentinelTray.dll (C++)\n      в”ңв”Җ System tray integration\n      в”ңв”Җ Notification handling\n      в”ңв”Җ Quick action implementation\n      в””в”Җ Status display\n```\n\n### 2.2 Data Architecture\n\n**2.2.1 Database Schema**\n```\nDatabase Schema (SQLite):\nв”ңв”Җ Threats Table\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ threat_id (INTEGER PRIMARY KEY)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ threat_name (TEXT)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ threat_type (TEXT)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ threat_severity (INTEGER)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ detection_time (TIMESTAMP)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ file_path (TEXT)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ file_hash (TEXT)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ action_taken (TEXT)\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ resolved (BOOLEAN)\nв”ңв”Җ Scans Table\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ scan_id (INTEGER PRIMARY KEY)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ scan_type (TEXT)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ start_time (TIMESTAMP)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ end_time (TIMESTAMP)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ files_scanned (INTEGER)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ threats_found (INTEGER)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ scan_duration (INTEGER)\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ scan_status (TEXT)\nв”ңв”Җ Quarantine Table\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ quarantine_id (INTEGER PRIMARY KEY)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ original_path (TEXT)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ quarantine_path (TEXT)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ file_hash (TEXT)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ threat_name (TEXT)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ quarantine_time (TIMESTAMP)\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ file_size (INTEGER)\nв”ңв”Җ Updates Table\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ update_id (INTEGER PRIMARY KEY)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ update_type (TEXT)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ update_version (TEXT)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ update_time (TIMESTAMP)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ update_status (TEXT)\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ update_size (INTEGER)\nв”ңв”Җ Settings Table\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ setting_id (INTEGER PRIMARY KEY)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ setting_key (TEXT)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ setting_value (TEXT)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ setting_type (TEXT)\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ last_modified (TIMESTAMP)\nв”ңв”Җ Events Table\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ event_id (INTEGER PRIMARY KEY)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ event_type (TEXT)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ event_time (TIMESTAMP)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ event_data (TEXT)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ event_severity (INTEGER)\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ event_source (TEXT)\nв””в”Җ Performance Table\n   в”ңв”Җ perf_id (INTEGER PRIMARY KEY)\n   в”ңв”Җ metric_name (TEXT)\n   в”ңв”Җ metric_value (REAL)\n   в”ңв”Җ metric_time (TIMESTAMP)\n   в””в”Җ metric_source (TEXT)\n```\n\n**2.2.2 File Structure**\n```\nFile Structure:\nC:\\Program Files\\SENTINEL\\\nв”ңв”Җ bin\\\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ hypervisor_core.dll\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ hypervisor_driver.sys\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ detection_engine.dll\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ ai_engine.dll\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ gaming_engine.dll\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ network_engine.dll\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ SentinelProtectionService.exe\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ SentinelUpdateService.exe\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ SentinelGamingService.exe\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ SentinelUIService.exe\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ SentinelScanner.exe\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ SentinelAIWorker.exe\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ SentinelNetworkMonitor.exe\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ SentinelTray.exe\nв”ңв”Җ data\\\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ sentinel.db (SQLite database)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ signatures.db (Encrypted)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ ai_models.db (Encrypted)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ game_profiles.db (Encrypted)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ firewall_rules.db (Encrypted)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ config.toml (Configuration)\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ logs\\\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ protection.log\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ updates.log\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ gaming.log\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ network.log\nв”Ӯ     в””в”Җ errors.log\nв”ңв”Җ models\\\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ threat_detection_model.pt (PyTorch model)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ anomaly_detection_model.pt\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ behavioral_analysis_model.pt\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ threat_prediction_model.pt\nв”ңв”Җ ui\\\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Sentinel.exe (Electron app)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ resources\\\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ icons\\\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ images\\\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ fonts\\\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ locales\\\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ en-US\\\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ pl-PL\nв”Ӯ     в””в”Җ de-DE\nв”ңв”Җ quarantine\\\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ [Quarantined files]\nв””в”Җ updates\\\n   в”ңв”Җ temp\\\n   в””в”Җ cache\\\n```\n\n## 3. Dependencies: torch, torchvision, numpy, pandas, scikit-learn\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Features: CNN, LSTM, attention mechanisms, federated learning\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Build: pip, poetry, pyproject.toml\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Detection Engine: C++23 + YARA 4.3\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Dependencies: yara, libyara, boost, spdlog\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Features: YARA rules, heuristic analysis, behavioral analysis\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ protection, optimization\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Build: CMake 3.28+, vcpkg, MSVC 2022\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Network Engine: Rust 1.75+ (Tokio async runtime)\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Dependencies: tokio, pcap, serde, Marketing Campaign Plan\n\n### 2.1 Marketing Strategy\n\n```\nMarketing Strategy:\nв”ңв”Җ Target Segments\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Primary: Hardcore Gamers (40%)\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Age: 18-35\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ                     в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Exploratory testing                                 в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ   в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Ad-hoc testing                                      в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Defect Management                                       в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Bug reporting                                       в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Bug tracking                                        в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Bug verification                                    в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ   в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Bug closure                                         в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Test Reporting                                          в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Test summary reports                                 в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Quality metrics                                      в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Trend analysis                                       в”Ӯ\nв”Ӯ     в””в”Җ Recommendations                                      в”Ӯ\nв””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ\n```\n\n### 2.2 Testing Strategy\n\n**2.2.1 Testing Pyramid**\n```\nTesting Pyramid:\nв”ңв”Җ Unit Tests (70%)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Purpose: Test individual components\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Tools: Google Test (C++), Rust Testing, pytest (Python)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Coverage: >80% code coverage\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Execution: Automated, every commit\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Duration: <5 minutes\nв”ңв”Җ Integration Tests (20%)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Purpose: Test component interactions\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Tools: Custom integration framework\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Coverage: All critical paths\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Execution: Automated, every build\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Duration: <30 minutes\nв”ңв”Җ End-to-End Tests (5%)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Purpose: Test complete user workflows\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Tools: Selenium, Cypress, Playwright\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Coverage: Critical user journeys\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Execution: Automated, nightly\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Duration: <2 hours\nв””в”Җ Manual Tests (5%)\n   в”ңв”Җ Purpose: Exploratory testing, UX testing\n   в”ңв”Җ Tools: Manual testing, user testing\n   в”ңв”Җ Coverage: Edge cases, new features\n   в”ңв”Җ Execution: Manual, as needed\n   в””в”Җ Duration: Variable\n```\n\n**2.2.2 Test Types**\n```\nTest Types:\nв”ңв”Җ Functional Testing\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Unit testing\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Integration testing\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ System testing\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Acceptance testing\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Regression testing\nв”ңв”Җ Performance Testing\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Load testing\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Stress testing\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Scalability testing\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Endurance testing\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Spike testing\nв”ңв”Җ Security Testing\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Vulnerability scanning\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Penetration testing\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Security audit\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Compliance testing\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Fuzzing\nв”ңв”Җ Compatibility Testing\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ OS compatibility (Windows 10, 11)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Hardware compatibility (Intel, AMD, ARM)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Software compatibility (browsers, games)\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Network compatibility (different ISPs)\nв””в”Җ Usability Testing\n   в”ңв”Җ User testing\n   в”ңв”Җ Accessibility testing\n   в”ңв”Җ UX testing\n   в”ңв”Җ A/B testing\n   в””в”Җ Beta testing\n```\n\n### 2.3 Quality Metrics\n\n```\nQuality Metrics:\nв”ңв”Җ Code Quality\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Code coverage: >80%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Code complexity: <10 (cyclomatic complexity)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Code duplication: <5%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Technical debt: <20 hours\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Code review approval rate: >90%\nв”ңв”Җ Defect Metrics\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Defect density: <1 defect per 1000 LOC\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Defect leakage: <5% (from QA to production)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Critical defects: 0 in production\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ High defects: <5 in production\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Defect resolution time: <48 hours\nв”ңв”Җ Test Metrics\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Test coverage: >80%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Test pass rate: >95%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Test execution time: <2 hours\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Automated test ratio: >70%\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Test maintenance time: <10% of development time\nв”ңв”Җ Release Quality\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Release success rate: >95%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Rollback rate: <5%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Post-release defects: <10\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Release cycle time: <2 weeks\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Release confidence: >90%\nв””в”Җ Customer Quality\n   в”ңв”Җ Customer-reported defects: <100/month\n   в”ңв”Җ Customer satisfaction: >90%\n   в”ңв”Җ NPS score: >50\n   в”ңв”Җ Churn rate: <5%\n   в””в”Җ Support ticket rate: <5%\n```\n\n## 3. 3.2 Key Metrics and Dashboards\n\n**3.2.1 Technical Metrics Dashboard**\n```\nTechnical Metrics Dashboard:\nв”ңв”Җ System Health\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Uptime: 99.9%+\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Response time: <100ms (p95)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Error rate: <0.1%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Throughput: >1000 req/s\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Availability: 99.9%+\nв”ңв”Җ Resource Utilization\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ CPU usage: <70%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Memory usage: <80%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Disk usage: <70%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Network usage: <70%\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ I/O usage: <70%\nв”ңв”Җ Application Performance\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ API response time: <50ms (p95)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Database query time: <10ms (p95)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Cache hit rate: >90%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Page load time: <2s (p95)\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Transaction success rate: >99.9%\nв””в”Җ Security Metrics\n   в”ңв”Җ Threats blocked: >1000/day\n   в”ңв”Җ False positives: <0.1%\n   в”ңв”Җ Detection rate: >99%\n   в”ңв”Җ Security incidents: 0\n   в””в”Җ Vulnerabilities: 0 critical\n```\n\n**3.2.2 Business Metrics Dashboard**\n```\nBusiness Metrics Dashboard:\nв”ңв”Җ User Metrics\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Active users: 10K+ (Month 6)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ New users: 5K+/month\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ User retention: >80% (30-day)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ User engagement: >60% DAU/MAU\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ User satisfaction: >90%\nв”ңв”Җ Revenue Metrics\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ MRR: $200K+ (Month 12)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ ARR: $1M+ (Year 1)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ ARPU: $20+/month\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ CAC: $50\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ LTV: $300\nв”ңв”Җ Product Metrics\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Feature adoption: >70%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Daily active users: >60%\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Session duration: >10 minutes\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Page views per session: >5\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Conversion rate: >5%\nв””в”Җ Support Metrics\n   в”ңв”Җ Ticket volume: <100/day\n   в”ңв”Җ First response time: <1 hour\n   в”ңв”Җ Resolution time: <24 hours\n   в”ңв”Җ Customer satisfaction: >90%\n   в””в”Җ NPS score: >50\n```\n\n### 3.3 Alerting and Incident Management\n\n```\nAlerting Strategy:\nв”ңв”Җ Alert Severity Levels\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Critical (P1): Immediate action required (24/7)\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ System down\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Data breach\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Security incident\nв”Ӯ   в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Critical bug\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ High (P2): Action required within 1 hour (24/7)\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Performance degradation\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ High error rate\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Resource exhaustion\nв”Ӯ   в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Security vulnerability\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Medium (P3): Action required within 4 hours (business hours)\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Minor performance issue\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Elevated error rate\nв”Ӯ   в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Resource warning\nв”Ӯ   в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Non-critical bug\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Low (P4): Action required within 24 hours (business hours)\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Informational alert\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Minor issue\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Resource trend\nв”Ӯ     в””в”Җ Optimization opportunity\nв”ңв”Җ Alert Channels\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ PagerDuty / Opsgenie (Critical, High)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Slack (Medium, Low)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Email (All)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ SMS (Critical)\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Phone call (Critical)\nв””в”Җ Alert Escalation\n   в”ңв”Җ Level 1: On-call engineer (5 minutes)\n   в”ңв”Җ Level 2: Team lead (15 minutes)\n   в”ңв”Җ Level 3: Engineering manager (30 minutes)\n   в””в”Җ Level 4: CTO (1 hour)\n```\n\n## 4. Incident Response Procedures\n\n### 4.1 Incident Response Team\n\n```\nIncident Response Team:\nв”ңв”Җ Incident Commander (IC)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Responsibilities\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Lead incident Skills\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Leadership\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Communication\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Technical knowledge\nв”Ӯ     в””в”Җ Decision-making\nв”ңв”Җ Technical Lead (TL)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Responsibilities\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ (CL)\nв”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Responsibilities\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Manage internal communications\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Manage external communications\nв”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Prepare announcements\nв”Ӯ   в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Handle measures\nв”Ӯ   в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Conduct security investigation\nв”Ӯ   в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Document security findings\nв”Ӯ  в””в”Җ Skills\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Security expertise\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Forensics\nв”Ӯ     в”ңв”Җ Investigation\nв”Ӯ     в””в”Җ Documentation\nв””в”Җ Support Lead (SPL)\n   в”ңв”Җ Responsibilities\n   в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Manage customer communications\n   в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ Coordinate support team\n   в”Ӯ
